    Summary statistics section: 
    ===========================
    This section includes the highlight statistics for a quick lookup  
        Show general system information from CLI command /info/sys/general   
        Show enabled software features from CLI command /info/swkey   
        Shows users currently logged in via different SSH/TELNET/SNMP from CLI command /who   
        Show the base MAC, PIP MAC and VIRTs MAC
        Show 64 seconds MP CPU utilization from CLI Command /stats/mp/cpu
        Show 4 and 64 seconds All SPs CPU utilization and memory stats from CLI Command /stats/sp/allutils
        Show session table statistics from CLI Command /stats/slb/maint
        Show peak data information from CLI Command /stats/slb/peakinfo
        Show the panic dump available in flash memory from CLI Command /maint/lsdmp
        Show the list of available core dump files from CLI command /maint/coredump/list
        Show High Availability information from CLI Command /info/l3/ha

    Tsdmp complete output: 
    ======================
    CLI Command /info/dump includes:
            CLI Command /info/sys/dump: Dump all system information
            CLI Command /info/sys/cyberc: Show cyber controller info
            CLI Command /info/sys/sslchip: Show SSL chip information
            CLI Command /info/l2/dump: Dump all Layer 2 information
            CLI Command /info/l3/dump: Dump all layer 3 information
            CLI Command /info/link: Show link status
            CLI Command /info/port: Show port information
            CLI Command /info/sys/capacity: Show switch capacity information
            CLI Command /info/bwm/cont: Show Bandwidth Management Contract information
            CLI Command /info/slb/dump: Show all layer 4 information
            CLI Command /info/swkey: Show enabled software features
            CLI Command /info/slb/synatk: Show SYN attack detection information
            CLI Command /info/slb/gslb/dump: Show all Global SLB information
            CLI Command /info/sec/dump: Show all security information
    CLI Command /maint/debug/spfdb: Show All SPs fdb tables
    CLI Command /info/slb/ddstore/persist/dump: Show all persistency entries
    CLI Command /stats/dump: Dump all stats
    DNSSEC Information - no CLI command
    CLI Command /maint/debug/health/runtime: Show per instance run-time health check
    CLI Command /maint/debug/connections/stats: Display connection module statistics
    CLI Command /maint/debug/connections/fdprint: Display monitored mgmt port fd/sockid
    CLI Command /maint/debug/appwall/awver: See appwall version
    CLI Command /maint/debug/tbuf: Show MP trace buffer
    CLI Command /maint/debug/ax/axoos/dump: Show AX Out Of Sync Statistics
    Software build information
    CLI Command /cfg/dump: Dump current configuration to script file
    CLI Command /maint/debug/flowdir: Display Flow Director stats
    CLI Command /maint/debug/appwall/awstat: Check Appwall process status
    CLI Command /maint/debug/mpschedule/cur: Display current  CPU scheduling percentage for MP
    CLI Command /maint/applog/getlevel: Get the log level set in AE for all or specific modules
    CLI Command /stats/counters/getevents: Show the list of current events counters
    CLI Command /stats/counters/geterrors: Show the list of current errors counters
    CLI Command /maint/geo/dump: Display Geolocation cache table
    CLI Command /maint/geo/index: Display the current GeoDB file index in use
    CLI Command /maint/geo/info: Display the current GeoDB file build date
    URLF information
    CLI Command /maint/debug/dxp/dxmlstat: Display DXML builder status
    CLI Command /maint/debug/dnsdmp: Display DNS Cache Table
    CLI Command /cfg/slb/appshape/script APM_script/cur: Display the current APM_script
 GEL is not enable on this Alteon:==========================================================================================================

when HTTP_REQUEST {
  # look for the 'sptier0' string
  set uri [HTTP::uri]
  set sptier0_index [string first sptier0 $uri 0] 
  if { $sptier0_index != -1 } {

    if { [string first APM.js $uri $sptier0_index] != -1 } {
      HTTP::respond 200 content $static::JS "Content-Type" "text/javascript"
      return
    }

    if { [string first Tier0.html $uri $sptier0_index] != -1 } {
      set xff [HTTP::header value "X-Forwarded-For"]
      if { $xff != "" } {
        set client_ip [lindex [split $xff ", "] 0]
      } else {
        set client_ip [IP::client_addr]
      }
      HTTP::header insert "X-RIP" $client_ip
      set rff [split [HTTP::header value "X-SharePath-RUM-Referrer"] "/"]
      HTTP::header replace "X-SharePath-RUM-Referrer" [join [lreplace $rff 2 2 [server address [lindex $rff 2]]] "/"]
    }
    host apm
  }
}

#define LNK_NEGOTIATE_AUTO  0x00002000  /* autonegotiation 'auto': define auto negotiation according to medium */  
#define LNK_FULL_DUPLEX     0x00100000  /* status/config: full duplex */  
#define LNK_HALF_DUPLEX     0x00200000  /* status/config: half duplex */  
#define LNK_TX_FLOW_CTL_Y   0x00400000  /* status/config: do TX flow control */  
#define LNK_RX_FLOW_CTL_Y   0x00800000  /* status/config: do RX flow control */  
#define LNK_ENABLE          0x40000000  /* status/config: enable/disable link */  
#define LNK_UP              0x80000000  /* status: link is operational */  

SFP media types:
UND_PORT_MEDIA_INIT:            Initial SFP   
UND_PORT_MEDIA_NONE:            No SFP
UND_PORT_MEDIA_UNKNOWN:         Unknown SFP
UND_PORT_MEDIA_SFP_COPPER:      		Rate: 1Gbps, Type: Copper, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: On
UND_PORT_MEDIA_SFP_FIBER:       		Rate: 1Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: On/Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_SFP_PLUS_COPPER_DAC: 	Rate: 10Gbps, Type: Copper, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_SFP_PLUS_COPPER_RJ45: 	Rate: 10Gbps, Type: Copper, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_SFP_PLUS_FIBER:  		Rate: 10Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_XFP_FIBER:       		Rate: 10Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_SFP_25G_SR_FIBER:       Rate: 25Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_SFP_25G_LR_FIBER:       Rate: 25Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_QSFP_FIBER:      		Rate: 40Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_QSFP_COPPER:     		Rate: 40Gbps, Type: Copper, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_QSFP28_LR4_FIBER:    	Rate: 100Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_QSFP28_SR4_FIBER:    	Rate: 100Gbps, Type: Fiber, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
UND_PORT_MEDIA_QSFP_PLUS:       		Rate: 100Gbps, Type: Copper, Duplex: Full, Auto Negotiation: Off
